Answer: The problem is that you are running the management plugin on the same node as the cluster.  You need to run it on a separate node.  This is explained in the [RabbitMQ documentation]({error_logger,{{rabbit,server_boot},{error,{'EXIT',{{badmatch,{error,shutdown}},
